TL;DR: Ceci是一个关怀共情的C语言IDE，旨在通过情感支持而非直接代码生成来帮助新手程序员。与VSCode+ChatGPT相比，Ceci在错误修正方面被认为更有帮助，但在学习效果、工作负荷等方面无显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式AI在软件开发中的普及，存在过度依赖和批判性思维减弱的风险。研究旨在探索如何通过共情编程环境支持新手程序员的学习过程，而不是直接生成代码。

Method: 开发了Ceci（Caring Empathic C IDE），并与VSCode+ChatGPT进行对比研究。11名参与者完成编码任务，使用NASA-TLX工作负荷评估和可用性调查问卷进行评估。

Result: 样本量较小（n=11），实验组和对照组在感知效果、学习和工作负荷方面无显著差异。但Ceci用户在错误修正方面的感知帮助性显著更高（p=0.0220）。

Conclusion: 单纯的共情响应可能不足以改善学习结果、感知或减少工作负荷。研究为未来探索提供了基础框架，需要更大样本、多样化任务和更好的界面整合。

Abstract: As generative AI becomes integral to software development, the risk of over-reliance and diminished critical thinking grows. This study introduces "Ceci," our Caring Empathic C IDE designed to support novice programmers by prioritizing learning and emotional support over direct code generation. The researchers conducted a comparative pilot study between Ceci and VSCode + ChatGPT [9, 40]. Participants completed a coding task and were evaluated using the NASA-TLX workload assessment and a post-test usability survey. Although the sample size was small (n = 11), results show that there is no significant difference in perceived effectiveness, learning and workload between the Experimental Ceci group and the Control group, though Ceci users reported significantly greater perceived helpfulness in error correction (p = 0.0220). These findings suggest that empathic responses may not be sufficient on their own to enhance the learner's outcomes, perceptions, or reduce workload. Overall, this study provides a foundational framework for future research. Such research should explore larger sample sizes, diverse programming tasks, and additional empathic features to better understand the potential of empathic programming environments in supporting novice programmers; they must also ensure that the empathic features are well-integrated in the user interface.

### [243] [Cascaded Code Editing: Large-Small Model Collaboration for Effective and Efficient Code Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19201)
*Chaozheng Wang,Zezhou Yang,Shuzheng Gao,Cuiyun Gao,Zongjie Li,Yichen Li,Ting Peng,Hailiang Huang,Yuetang Deng,Michael R. Lyu*

Method: 两阶段级联方法：1) 编辑草图生成（大模型）：生成简洁修改草图；2) 编辑草图应用（小模型）：将草图整合到原代码生成最终编辑代码

Abstract: Code editing constitutes a fundamental practice in software development, wherein developers modify existing codebases according to natural language requirements. Accurate code editing necessitates a comprehensive understanding of both the existing codebase and the modification requirements. Although large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated promising performance in code editing tasks, they suffer from substantial inefficiency by generating entire modified files that largely consist of unchanged code. While smaller models could potentially address this inefficiency, they typically lack the capacity to effectively comprehend long code contexts required for accurate editing. To ensure both effectiveness and efficiency, we propose to decompose code editing into a two-stage cascade: \textbf{edit sketch generation}, wherein a large model first produces concise sketches representing the requisite modifications (the more challenging phase), and \textbf{edit sketch application}, wherein a smaller model integrates these sketches into the original code to produce the final output edited code (the simpler phase). This cascaded design reduces the number of tokens generated by the large model, as the majority of the output is handled by the smaller, more efficient model, thereby enhancing overall efficiency. However, the effectiveness of this approach is constrained by current small models' limited capabilities in handling long-context scenarios and cross-file dependencies, which are essential for accurate sketch application in real-world codebases. ### [244] [iCoRe: An Iterative Correlation-Aware Retriever for Bug Reproduction Test Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19224)
*Junyi Wang,Jialun Cao,Zhongxin Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: iCoRe提出了一种迭代的、相关性感知的上下文检索方法，用于从问题描述自动生成bug重现测试，通过区分源代码和测试用例的检索需求，结合语义和函数调用关系，并引入检索与生成阶段的反馈循环，显著提高了bug重现的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based bug重现测试生成方法在检索阶段存在三个关键问题：1) 对源代码和测试用例采用统一检索策略，忽视了它们不同的检索需求；2) 仅关注语义相似性而忽略函数调用关系，导致检索到不相关的上下文；3) 缺乏从生成阶段的反馈循环，无法基于执行结果优化上下文。这些问题导致检索到的上下文质量低，从而影响bug重现的准确性。

Method: iCoRe是一种迭代的、相关性感知的上下文检索方法，明确关注三种关键相关性：1) 源代码和测试用例之间的相关性，需要差异化检索；2) 文本语义和函数调用结构之间的相关性，用于准确的相关性评估；3) 检索和生成阶段之间的相关性，实现迭代反馈和优化。该方法与LLM-based BRT生成器集成，在检索过程中考虑这些相关性。

Result: 在SWT-bench Lite和TDD-bench Verified基准测试上的实验结果显示，iCoRe分别达到了42.0%和52.8%的Fail-to-Pass率，相比现有检索方法实现了19.7%-31.7%的相对改进。

Conclusion: iCoRe通过考虑源代码与测试用例的差异化检索需求、结合语义和函数调用关系、以及引入检索与生成阶段的反馈循环，显著提高了bug重现测试生成的上下文质量，从而提升了bug重现的准确性。

Abstract: Automatically generating bug reproduction tests (BRT) from issue descriptions is crucial for software maintenance. LLM-based approaches have shown great potential for this task. Their effectiveness heavily relies on retrieving high-quality context from the codebase. The retrieval phase of existing approaches relies on either traditional methods like BM25 or LLM-driven strategies. LLM-based retrieval strategies typically equip an LLM with tools to autonomously explore the repository or select the most relevant files and code snippets from a provided list as context. However, these retrieval methods suffer from three key limitations: 1) They often employ a unified strategy for retrieving both source code and test cases, overlooking their distinct retrieval requirements. 2) They focus solely on semantic similarity while ignoring function call relationships, leading to irrelevant context. 3) The retrieval lacks a feedback loop from the generation phase, preventing it from refining the context based on execution results. These limitations collectively result in low-quality context, thereby hindering the accuracy of bug reproduction. To address these challenges, we propose iCoRe, an iterative, correlation-aware context retrieval approach explicitly aware of three key correlations: 1) between source code and test cases, which requires differentiated retrieval, 2) between textual semantics and function call structures for accurate relevance assessment, and 3) between the retrieval and generation phases, which enables iterative feedback and refinement. To evaluate iCoRe, we integrate it with an LLM-based BRT generator and conduct a comprehensive evaluation on the SWT-bench Lite and TDD-bench Verified benchmarks. Experimental results show that our method achieves a Fail-to-Pass rate of 42.0% and 52.8% respectively, representing 19.7%-31.7% relative improvements over existing retrieval methods.

### [245] [DebugRepair: Enhancing LLM-Based Automated Program Repair via Self-Directed Debugging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19305)
*Linhao Wu,Yifei Pei,Zhen Yang,Kainan Li,Zhonghang Lu,Hao Tan,Xiran Lyu,Jia Li,Yizhou Chen,Pengyu Xue,Kunwu Zheng,Dan Hao*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DebugRepair：基于LLM的自动程序修复框架，通过模拟调试收集中间运行时证据，提升补丁质量

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于反馈的APR方法主要依赖结果级失败症状（如堆栈跟踪），这些信息显示失败如何被观察到，但未能暴露对根本原因分析至关重要的中间运行时状态。这导致LLM在没有足够运行时证据的情况下推断错误原因，产生错误补丁。

Method: 提出DebugRepair框架，包含三个组件：1) 测试语义净化 - 减少噪声测试上下文；2) 模拟插桩 - 通过有针对性的调试语句收集运行时跟踪，并具有基于规则的备用方案；3) 调试驱动的对话修复 - 利用先前尝试和新观察到的运行时状态逐步细化候选补丁。

Result: 在Java和Python的三个基准测试上评估，DebugRepair在15种方法中达到最先进性能。使用GPT-3.5时，在Defects4J上正确修复224个错误，比先前最佳LLM方法提升26.2%。使用DeepSeek-V3时，正确修复295个Defects4J错误，比第二佳基线多59个。在五个额外骨干LLM上，DebugRepair比原始设置提升修复性能51.3%。

Conclusion: DebugRepair通过引入中间运行时证据收集的模拟调试，显著提升了基于LLM的自动程序修复效果，所有组件均被证明有效。

Abstract: Automated Program Repair (APR) has benefited from the code understanding and generation capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). Existing feedback-based APR methods iteratively refine candidate patches using test execution feedback and have shown promising results. However, most rely on outcome-level failure symptoms, such as stack traces, which show how failures are observed but fail to expose the intermediate runtime states critical for root-cause analysis. As a result, LLMs often infer bug causes without sufficient runtime evidence, leading to incorrect patches. To address this limitation, we propose DebugRepair, a self-directed debugging framework for LLM-based APR. DebugRepair enhances patch refinement with intermediate runtime evidence collected through simulated debugging. It consists of three components: test semantic purification, simulated instrumentation, and debugging-driven conversational repair. Together, they reduce noisy test context, collect runtime traces through targeted debugging statements with rule-based fallback, and progressively refine candidate patches using prior attempts and newly observed runtime states. We evaluate DebugRepair on three benchmarks across Java and Python. Experiments show that DebugRepair achieves state-of-the-art performance against 15 approaches. With GPT-3.5, it correctly fixes 224 bugs on Defects4J, outperforming prior SOTA LLM-based methods by 26.2%. With DeepSeek-V3, it correctly fixes 295 Defects4J bugs, surpassing the second-best baseline by 59 bugs. Across five additional backbone LLMs, DebugRepair improves repair performance by 51.3% over vanilla settings. Ablation studies further confirm the effectiveness of all components.

*Tobias Kiecker,Jan Arne Sparka,Martin Reuter,Albert Ziegler,Lars Grunske*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CASCADE是一个利用大语言模型从文档生成单元测试来检测代码与文档不一致性的工具，通过双重验证机制（现有代码失败而文档生成代码通过）来最小化误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码与文档不一致是软件开发中常见但常被忽视的问题，会导致API用户困惑、引入新bug并增加维护成本。现有自动化解决方案存在误报问题，浪费开发时间并阻碍实际应用。

Method: CASCADE使用LLM从自然语言文档生成单元测试，同时从文档生成代码进行交叉验证。只有当现有代码测试失败而文档生成代码通过相同测试时，才报告不一致性，从而最小化误报。

Result: 在71个不一致和814个一致的代码-文档对数据集上评估，并在Java、C#和Rust项目中发现了13个先前未知的不一致性，其中10个已被修复，证明了工具的精确性和实际应用价值。

Conclusion: CASCADE通过LLM生成测试和代码的双重验证机制，有效检测代码-文档不一致性并显著减少误报，在实际项目中展示了实用性和精确性。

Abstract: Maintaining consistency between code and documentation is a crucial yet frequently overlooked aspect of software development. Even minor mismatches can confuse API users, introduce new bugs, and increase overall maintenance effort. This creates demand for automated solutions that can assist developers in identifying code-documentation inconsistencies. However, since automatic reports still require human confirmation, false positives carry serious consequences: wasting developer time and discouraging practical adoption.
  We introduce CASCADE (Consistency Analysis for Source Code And Documentation through Execution), a novel tool for detecting inconsistencies with a strong emphasis on reducing false positives. CASCADE leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) to generate unit tests directly from natural-language documentation. Since these tests are derived from the documentation, any failure during execution indicates a potential mismatch between the documented and actual behavior of the code. To minimize false positives, CASCADE also generates code from the documentation to cross-check the generated tests. By design, an inconsistency is reported only when two conditions are met: the existing code fails a test, while the code generated from the documentation passes the same test.
  We evaluated CASCADE on a novel dataset of 71 inconsistent and 814 consistent code-documentation pairs drawn from open-source Java projects. Further, we applied CASCADE to additional Java, C#, and Rust repositories, where we uncovered 13 previously unknown inconsistencies, of which 10 have subsequently been fixed, demonstrating both CASCADE's precision and its applicability to real-world codebases.

TL;DR: ReCent-Prover是一个基于LLM的推理中心化证明代理，通过验证与反思、基于规划的检索两项技术，在相同LLM调用预算下将CoqStoq基准上的定理证明数量相对提升22.58%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有证明代理未能充分利用现代LLM在高层规划和自我批判方面的推理能力，它们主要生成策略而缺乏对证明计划的战略思考和对自己建议的批判性评估。

Method: 1. 验证与反思：让LLM审查自己生成的策略，当反思识别潜在错误时合成失败摘要，提前过滤可能误用的策略。2. 基于规划的检索：基于LLM生成的证明计划而非子目标相似性进行检索，检索与预期证明策略一致的引理和证明。

Conclusion: 推理中心化的设计显著增强了自动定理证明能力，验证与反思、基于规划的检索是有效的技术，即使增加了LLM调用次数，但在相同预算下仍能取得显著性能提升。

Abstract: Automated theorem proving is fundamental to formal methods, and the recent trend is to integrate large language models (LLMs) and proof assistants to form effective proof agents. While existing proof agents show promising performance, they inadequately leverage reasoning capabilities of modern LLMs in high-level planning and self-critique. We argue that proof agents should not merely generate tactics but also reason strategically about proof plans and critically evaluate their own proposals.
  This paper introduces ReCent-Prover, a reasoning-centric LLM-based proof agent for Rocq that addresses two critical limitations in current systems. First, we present validation with reflection, enabling LLMs to scrutinize their generated tactics and synthesize failure summaries when reflection identifies potential errors, filtering out potentially misapplied tactics earlier. Second, we propose retrieval with planning, which conditions retrieval on LLM-generated proof plans rather than subgoal similarity, retrieving lemmas and proofs that align with the anticipated proof strategy. Both techniques increase the number of invocations of LLMs. However, when evaluated on the CoqStoq benchmark, even under the same budget of LLM invocations, ReCent-Prover achieves a 22.58% relative improvement in the number of proved theorems over the previous state-of-the-art, demonstrating that our reasoning-centric design significantly enhances automated theorem proving capabilities.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kubernetes现有的水平Pod自动扩展器（HPA）基于CPU利用率扩展，无法直接测量Node.js事件循环饱和度；KEDA虽然支持更丰富的触发器但仍采用反应式控制循环，检测到过载后才扩展，导致系统可能已经降级

Method: 提出预测性扩展算法，基于负载预测提前扩展；使用集群级聚合指标消除扩展动作对指标的反馈循环；定义指标模型和五阶段管道，将原始指标数据转换为清洁预测信号

Result: 在稳态斜坡和突发尖峰负载测试中，算法保持每个实例负载接近目标阈值；稳态斜坡下中位延迟为26ms，而KEDA为154ms，HPA为522ms

Conclusion: 预测性扩展算法通过提前预测负载变化并基于集群级聚合指标进行扩展，显著改善了Node.js工作负载在Kubernetes中的扩展性能，避免了反应式扩展的延迟问题

Abstract: Kubernetes offers two default paths for scaling Node.js workloads, and both have structural limitations. The Horizontal Pod Autoscaler scales on CPU utilization, which does not directly measure event loop saturation: a Node.js pod can queue requests and miss latency SLOs while CPU reports moderate usage. KEDA extends HPA with richer triggers, including event-loop metrics, but inherits the same reactive control loop, detecting overload only after it has begun. By the time new pods start and absorb traffic, the system may already be degraded. Lowering thresholds shifts the operating point but does not change the dynamic: the scaler still reacts to a value it has already crossed, at the cost of permanent over-provisioning.
  We propose a predictive scaling algorithm that forecasts where load will be by the time new capacity is ready and scales proactively based on that forecast. Per-instance metrics are corrupted by the scaler's own actions: adding an instance redistributes load and changes every metric, even if external traffic is unchanged. We observe that operating on a cluster-wide aggregate that is approximately invariant under scaling eliminates this feedback loop, producing a stable signal suitable for short-term extrapolation.
  We define a metric model (a set of three functions that encode how a specific metric relates to scaling) and a five-stage pipeline that transforms raw, irregularly-timed, partial metric data into a clean prediction signal. In benchmarks against HPA and KEDA under steady ramp and sudden spike, the algorithm keeps per-instance load near the target threshold throughout. Under the steady ramp, median latency is 26ms, compared to 154ms for KEDA and 522ms for HPA.

</details>


### [253] [PlayCoder: Making LLM-Generated GUI Code Playable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19742)
*Zhiyuan Peng,Wei Tao,Xin Yin,Chenhao Ying,Yuan Luo,Yiwen Guo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了PlayEval基准测试和PlayCoder框架，用于评估和改进LLM生成GUI应用的能力，发现现有模型在生成逻辑正确的GUI应用方面表现很差，而PlayCoder能显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在代码生成方面表现良好，但在生成GUI应用（特别是游戏）方面的能力研究不足。现有基准测试主要通过测试用例评估正确性，这对于交互式、事件驱动的GUI应用不够充分，需要评估交互流程和UI逻辑。

Method: 1) 提出PlayEval基准测试，包含43个多语言GUI应用，覆盖6个主要类别；2) 提出Play@k评估指标，衡量k个候选代码中是否有能完整运行且无逻辑错误的；3) 开发PlayTester代理，基于LLM执行任务导向的GUI测试并自动检测逻辑违规；4) 提出PlayCoder框架，采用多智能体、仓库感知的方法，在闭环中生成、评估和迭代修复GUI应用代码。

Result: 实验显示，10个最先进的代码LLM虽然编译率高，但Play@3接近零，表明在生成逻辑正确的GUI应用方面存在重大缺陷。PlayCoder显著提升了开源和闭源模型的功能正确性和语义对齐，最高达到38.1% Exec@3和20.3% Play@3。案例研究显示它能发现传统指标遗漏的静默逻辑错误并通过针对性编辑修复。

Conclusion: 现有LLM在生成逻辑正确的GUI应用方面能力有限，需要专门的评估方法和改进框架。PlayEval基准测试和PlayCoder框架能有效评估和提升LLM生成GUI应用的能力，为这一重要但研究不足的领域提供了解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved strong results in code generation, but their ability to generate GUI applications, especially games, remains insufficiently studied. Existing benchmarks mainly evaluate correctness through test cases, which are inadequate for GUI applications because these systems are interactive, event-driven, and require correct state transitions across sequences of user actions. Their evaluation therefore should consider interaction flows and UI logic rather than only pass/fail outcomes. To study this problem, we introduce PlayEval, a repository-aware benchmark built from 43 multilingual GUI applications in Python, TypeScript, and JavaScript. Unlike prior GUI benchmarks that are difficult to adapt to desktop environments, PlayEval covers six major GUI application categories and directly supports code-generation evaluation. We further propose Play@k, a metric that measures whether at least one of *k* generated candidates can be played end-to-end without logical errors. To support reliable evaluation, we develop PlayTester, an LLM-based agent that performs task-oriented GUI playthroughs and detects logic violations automatically. Experiments on 10 state-of-the-art code LLMs show that, despite high compilation rates, they achieve near-zero Play@3, revealing major weaknesses in generating logically correct GUI applications. To address this limitation, we present PlayCoder, a multi-agent, repository-aware framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively repairs GUI application code in a closed loop. PlayCoder substantially improves both functional correctness and semantic alignment for open-source and closed-source models, reaching up to 38.1% Exec@3 and 20.3% Play@3. Case studies further show that it can uncover silent logic bugs missed by traditional metrics and fix them through targeted edits.

</details>

### [254] [From Tokens to Ties: Network and Discourse Analysis of Web3 Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18761)
*Valentina Kuskova,Dmitry Zaytsev*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 论文通过融合区块链链上交易和社交媒体链下活动的大数据分析，揭示Web3生态中不同参与角色如何塑造社区网络结构和话语动态，发现持有者主导的网络能演变为社会嵌入的生态系统，而交易者和投机者主导的网络则保持碎片化和交易性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上Web3生态系统主要被视为数字资产市场，但本研究认为它们更是网络化的社会空间，经济交易会催生持久的社会联系、共享叙事和集体身份。需要超越纯粹的经济或技术视角，理解Web3空间中价值、身份和不平等如何协商。

Method: 1. 大规模数据挖掘：融合链上区块链交易和链下社交媒体活动数据；2. 分析超过100个NFT收藏品；3. 网络分析识别不同生态系统角色（长期持有者、活跃交易者、短期投机者）；4. 话语分析社交媒体参与，研究叙事生产、可见性和持续互动。

Result: 1. 不同参与角色产生显著不同的网络拓扑结构、凝聚水平和影响力路径；2. 以持有行为为中心的社区能从交易网络演变为社会嵌入的生态系统，具有密集联系、去中心化影响力和持续文化参与特征；3. 交易者和投机者主导的网络保持碎片化和交易性；4. 叙事生产、可见性和持续互动在交易活动下降后仍能持续。

Conclusion: 通过将网络结构与话语动态联系起来，本研究提供了一个社会技术框架来理解Web3空间中价值、身份和不平等的协商过程。该方法为检测包容、排斥和代表性不平衡模式提供了可扩展的方法，推动了数字社区网络研究超越纯粹的经济或技术解释。

Abstract: This paper examines Web3 ecosystems not merely as markets for digital assets, but as networked social spaces where economic transactions give rise to enduring social ties, shared narratives, and collective identities. Leveraging large-scale data mining of fused on-chain blockchain transactions and off-chain social media activity, we analyze over one hundred NFT collections to uncover how different forms of participation structure community formation in decentralized environments. Using network analysis, we identify distinct ecosystem roles, such as long-term holders, active traders, and short-term speculators, and demonstrate how each produces markedly different network topologies, levels of cohesion, and pathways for influence. We complement this structural analysis with discourse analysis of social media engagement, revealing how narrative production, visibility, and sustained interaction persist even as transactional activity declines. Our findings show that communities centered on holding behavior evolve from transactional networks into socially embedded ecosystems characterized by dense ties, decentralized influence, and ongoing cultural participation, while trader- and speculator-dominated networks remain fragmented and transactional. By linking network structure with discursive dynamics, this study provides a sociotechnical framework for understanding how value, identity, and inequality are negotiated in Web3 spaces. The approach offers a scalable method for detecting patterns of inclusion, exclusion, and representational imbalance, advancing network-based research on digital communities beyond purely economic or technical accounts.

</details>


### [255] [Optimal Exploration of New Products under Assortment Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18800)
*Jackie Baek,Atanas Dinev,Thodoris Lykouris*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 平台在容量限制下通过品类决策学习新产品质量，研究发现：新产品应与顶级现有产品搭配展示；同时探索的新产品数量具有阈值结构；传统多臂老虎机算法在此场景下失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平台需要决定是否展示新产品以学习其质量（通过顾客购买后的评价），但探索成本高，因为新产品需求低于现有产品。需要找到最优的品类决策策略来最小化遗憾。

Method: 研究在线学习框架下平台容量受限的品类决策问题。新产品质量未知，通过社会学习（顾客评价）逐步揭示。分析两种关键决策：新产品单独展示还是与现有产品搭配；多个新产品是同时探索还是顺序探索。

Result: 1. 新产品应与顶级现有产品搭配展示，尽管这会降低新产品购买概率；2. 同时探索的新产品数量具有简单阈值结构，随新产品"潜力"增加，但与个体购买概率无关；3. UCB算法过度探索，Thompson Sampling算法探索不足，两者在此场景下均失效。

Conclusion: 平台学习新产品的最优策略具有结构性特征：搭配展示优于单独展示；同时探索数量由潜力决定而非购买概率；传统老虎机算法不适用此场景。研究为平台通过品类决策学习新产品提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study online learning for new products on a platform that makes capacity-constrained assortment decisions on which products to offer. For a newly listed product, its quality is initially unknown, and quality information propagates through social learning: when a customer purchases a new product and leaves a review, its quality is revealed to both the platform and future customers. Since reviews require purchases, the platform must feature new products in the assortment ("explore") to generate reviews to learn about new products. Such exploration is costly because customer demand for new products is lower than for incumbent products. We characterize the optimal assortments for exploration to minimize regret, addressing two questions. (1) Should the platform offer a new product alone or alongside incumbent products? The former maximizes the purchase probability of the new product but yields lower short-term revenue. Despite the lower purchase probability, we show it is always optimal to pair the new product with the top incumbent products. (2) With multiple new products, should the platform explore them simultaneously or one at a time? We show that the optimal number of new products to explore simultaneously has a simple threshold structure: it increases with the "potential" of the new products and, surprisingly, does not depend on their individual purchase probabilities. We also show that two canonical bandit algorithms, UCB and Thompson Sampling, both fail in this setting for opposite reasons: UCB over-explores while Thompson Sampling under-explores. Our results provide structural insights on how platforms should learn about new products through assortment decisions.

</details>


### [256] [Spatiotemporal Link Formation Prediction in Social Learning Networks Using Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18888)
*Ali Mohammadiasl,Bita Akram,Seyyedali Hosseinalipour,Rajeev Sahay*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出一个图神经网络框架，结合课堂内的时间演化和跨课堂的空间聚合来进行社会学习网络的链接预测，在教育环境中显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社会学习网络（SLNs）能捕捉教育环境中的学生互动，准确预测未来互动对于促进协作学习、及时干预和设计有效小组活动至关重要。传统链接预测方法通常针对一般在线社交网络，忽略了SLNs的复杂、非欧几里得和动态演化特性，在教育环境中效果有限。

Method: 提出一个图神经网络（GNN）框架，联合考虑课堂内的时间演化和跨课堂的空间聚合来进行SLNs的链接预测。具体分析了四个不同课堂的SLNs在（i）时间演化（不同时间点）、（ii）空间聚合（联合SLN分析）、（iii）课程期间不同时间点的不同空间聚合下的链接预测性能。

Result: 结果显示：随着课程时间推进，未来链接预测性能有统计显著的提升；聚合多个课堂的SLNs通常能提升模型性能，尤其在稀疏数据集中更明显；联合利用SLNs的时间演化和空间聚合显著优于单独分析课堂的传统基线方法。

Conclusion: 研究证明了具有教育意义的链接预测的有效性，对早期课程决策和课堂内外的可扩展学习分析具有直接应用价值，表明结合时间演化和空间聚合的GNN框架能显著提升教育环境中社会学习网络的链接预测性能。

Abstract: Social learning networks (SLNs) are graphical representations that capture student interactions within educational settings (e.g., a classroom), with nodes representing students and edges denoting interactions. Accurately predicting future interactions in these networks (i.e., link prediction) is crucial for enabling effective collaborative learning, supporting timely instructional interventions, and informing the design of effective group-based learning activities. However, traditional link prediction approaches are typically tuned to general online social networks (OSNs), often overlooking the complex, non-Euclidean, and dynamically evolving structure of SLNs, thus limiting their effectiveness in educational settings. In this work, we propose a graph neural network (GNN) framework that jointly considers the temporal evolution within classrooms and spatial aggregation across classrooms to perform link prediction in SLNs. Specifically, we analyze link prediction performance of GNNs over the SLNs of four distinct classrooms across their (i) temporal evolutions (varying time instances), (ii) spatial aggregations (joint SLN analysis), and (iii) varying spatial aggregations at varying temporal evolutions throughout the course. Our results indicate statistically significant performance improvements in the prediction of future links as the courses progress temporally. Aggregating SLNs from multiple classrooms generally enhances model performance as well, especially in sparser datasets. Moreover, we find that jointly leveraging both the temporal evolution and spatial aggregation of SLNs significantly outperforms conventional baseline approaches that analyze classrooms in isolation. Our findings demonstrate the efficacy of educationally meaningful link predictions, with direct implications for early-course decision-making and scalable learning analytics in and across classroom settings.

</details>


### [257] [When Transparency Falls Short: Auditing Platform Moderation During a High-Stakes Election](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19285)
*Benedetta Tessa,Gautam Kishore Shahi,Amaury Trujillo,Stefano Cresci*

Main category: cs.SI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究社交媒体平台在重大政治事件期间是否调整内容审核实践，利用《数字服务法案》透明度数据库首次大规模系统性地评估平台合规性和有效性。

Method: 分析欧洲八大社交媒体平台在2024年欧洲议会选举前后八个月内报告的15.8亿次内容审核行动，通过透明度数据库进行系统性研究。

Result: 平台在选举期间未表现出有意义的审核策略调整，自我报告的执行模式没有显著变化；透明度数据库启动一年后，平台的透明度和问责制问题仍然存在。

Conclusion: 当前自我监管方法存在局限性，需要更强有力的执法和更好的数据访问机制，以确保在线平台履行保护民主进程的责任。

Abstract: During major political events, social media platforms encounter increased systemic risks. However, it is still unclear if and how they adjust their moderation practices in response. The Digital Services Act Transparency Database provides-for the first time-an opportunity to systematically examine content moderation at scale, allowing researchers and policymakers to evaluate platforms' compliance and effectiveness, especially at high-stakes times. Here we analyze 1.58 billion self-reported moderation actions by the eight largest social media platforms in Europe over an eight-month period surrounding the 2024 European Parliament elections. We found that platforms did not exhibit meaningful signs of adaptation in moderation strategies as their self-reported enforcement patterns did not change significantly around the elections. This raises questions about whether platforms made any concrete adjustments, or whether the structure of the database may have masked them. On top of that, we reveal that initial concerns regarding platforms' transparency and accountability still persist one year after the launch of the Transparency Database. Our findings highlight the limits of current self-regulatory approaches and point to the need for stronger enforcement and better data access mechanisms to ensure that online platforms meet their responsibilities in protecting the democratic processes.

### [258] [Community Detection with the Canonical Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19291)
*Rudy Arthur*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 该论文将社区检测从无监督学习问题转化为假设检验问题，通过定义类似z分数的检验统计量和基于最大熵的零模型，评估特定社区结构相对于随机模型的证据强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统网络社区检测通常被视为无监督学习问题，使用通用算法对网络进行划分。但这种方法可能无法回答分析师关心的具体问题。作者认为应将社区检测视为假设检验问题，评估观察到的网络相对于零模型是否存在特定社区结构的证据。

Method: 定义了一个类似z分数的检验统计量，并基于规范系综中不同约束下的最大熵原理推导了多个零模型。通过比较观察网络与零模型的差异来检验特定社区结构的假设。

Result: 在真实和合成数据上验证了该方法，并与基于随机块模型的贝叶斯方法进行了对比。该方法能够为具体问题提供明确答案，比通用算法输出对分析师更有用。

Conclusion: 将社区检测视为假设检验问题的方法比传统无监督学习方法更具实用性，能够为分析师关心的具体问题提供明确的统计证据，而不是仅仅输出通用的社区划分结果。

Abstract: Network community detection is usually considered as an unsupervised learning problem. Given a network, the aim is to partition it using some general purpose algorithm. In this paper we instead treat community detection as a hypothesis testing problem. Given a network, we examine the evidence for specific community structure in the observed network compared to a null model. To do this we define an appropriate test statistic, analogous to a z-score, and several null models derived from maximising entropy under different constraints in the canonical ensemble. We demonstrate the application of this method on real and synthetic data and contrast our method to Bayesian approaches based on the stochastic block model. We demonstrate that this method gives definitive answers to concrete questions, which can be more useful to analysts than the output of a generic algorithm.

</details>


### [259] [The eigenvector centrality of hypergraphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19466)
*Changjiang Bu,Haotian Zeng,Qingying Zhang*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 该论文为非均匀超图定义了邻接张量，并提出了基于张量的特征向量中心性度量方法，统一了图、均匀超图和非均匀超图的中心性分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界中许多系统（如邮件网络和合著网络）产生的是非均匀超图，但现有中心性度量主要针对均匀超图或图。需要一种统一的方法来处理各种类型的超图，包括非均匀超图。

Method: 为超图定义邻接张量，并基于此张量提出特征向量中心性度量。该方法在均匀超图时退化为Benson的方法，在二元边时退化为图的特征向量中心性。

Result: 在多个真实世界超图数据集上的实验表明，与传统中心性度量相比，提出的方法提供了识别重要顶点的独特视角，并能有效识别它们。

Conclusion: 提出的超图特征向量中心性为分析非均匀超图提供了统一的数学框架，能够有效识别重要顶点，并兼容现有的图和平均匀超图中心性理论。

Abstract: A hypergraph is called uniform when every hyperedge contains the same number of vertices, otherwise, it is called non-uniform. In the real world, many systems give rise to non-uniform hypergraphs, such as email networks and co-authorship networks. A uniform hypergraph has a natural one-to-one correspondence with its adjacency tensor. In 2019, Benson proposed the eigenvector centrality of uniform hypergraphs via its adjacency tensor. In this paper, we define an adjacency tensor for hypergraphs and propose the eigenvector centrality for hypergraphs. When the hypergraph is uniform, our proposed eigenvector centrality reduces to Benson's. When each edge of the uniform hypergraph contains exactly two vertices, our proposed centrality reduces to the eigenvector centrality of graphs. We conducted experiments on several real-world hypergraph datasets. The results show that, compared to traditional centrality measures, the proposed centrality measure provides a unique perspective for identifying important vertices and can also effectively identify them.

</details>


### [260] [Hypergraph Mining via Proximity Matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19531)
*Junhao Bian,Yilin Bi,Tao Zhou*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出了一种连续值的超图邻近矩阵，替代传统的二元关联矩阵，能更准确捕捉节点与超边的关系，在链接预测、关键节点识别和社区检测任务中显著优于基准算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超图关联矩阵的二元性质不足以准确捕捉节点与超边关系的复杂性，特别是当不同超边包含节点数量差异巨大时，需要更精细的量化方法。

Method: 基于超图上的资源分配过程，提出了一种连续值的邻近矩阵来量化节点与超边之间的邻近度，替代传统的二元关联矩阵。

Result: 在大量真实世界超图上的实验表明，基于该邻近矩阵设计的简单算法在链接预测、关键节点识别和社区检测三个任务中均显著优于基准算法。

Conclusion: 提出的连续值邻近矩阵能更有效地表征超图中的高阶交互关系，为超图分析和挖掘提供了更强大的基础工具。

Abstract: Hypergraphs serve as an effective tool widely adopted to characterize higher-order interactions in complex systems. The most intuitive and commonly used mathematical instrument for representing a hypergraph is the incidence matrix, in which each entry is binary, indicating whether the corresponding node belongs to the corresponding hyperedge. Although the incidence matrix has become a foundational tool for hypergraph analysis and mining, we argue that its binary nature is insufficient to accurately capture the complexity of node-hyperedge relationships arising from the fact that different hyperedges can contain vastly different numbers of nodes. Accordingly, based on the resource allocation process on hypergraphs, we propose a continuous-valued matrix to quantify the proximity between nodes and hyperedges. To verify the effectiveness of the proposed proximity matrix, we investigate three important tasks in hypergraph mining: link prediction, vital nodes identification, and community detection. Experimental results on numerous real-world hypergraphs show that simply designed algorithms centered on the proximity matrix significantly outperform benchmark algorithms across these three tasks.

</details>

### [261] [Direction-Dependent Path Loss Modeling in Olive Orchards for Precision Agriculture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19427)
*Mohammad Rowhani Sistani,Katarzyna Kosek-Szott,Pierluigi Gallo*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出基于果园拓扑结构的无线传播模型，相比传统距离模型能更准确预测橄榄园中LoRa信号强度


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 果园中无线信号强度变化大，传统距离传播模型（如FSPL和ITU-R植被损耗模型）无法准确捕捉行结构橄榄园中沿行和跨行方向的信号衰减差异

Method: 提出基于拓扑结构的传播模型，考虑果园布局和无线电设备在种植结构中的相对位置，使用868 MHz LoRa技术进行实验验证，并与文献中的现有模型及提出的二维模型进行比较

Result: 所提方法比传统模型更接近实测RSSI数据，为结构化农业环境中的链路预算和网络规划提供了更可靠的基础

Conclusion: 针对行结构果园的拓扑感知传播模型能显著提高无线信号预测精度，适用于农业物联网应用中的网络规划

Abstract: Wireless links deployed in orchards often exhibit significant variability in the strength of the received signal that is not adequately captured by classical distance-based propagation models. In row-structured olive groves, signal attenuation differs markedly between along-row and cross-row propagation directions, leading to discrepancies when using omnidirectional propagation assumptions such as those adopted in the Free Space Path Loss (FSPL) model or ITU-R vegetation loss formulations. This paper proposes a topology-based propagation model that explicitly accounts for orchard layout and the relative positions of radio devices within the plantation structure. Experimental validation was conducted using LoRa technology operating at 868 MHz, and the results were compared with established models from the literature and with the proposed two-dimensional model. The proposed approach achieves a closer fit to measured RSSI data than conventional models, providing a more reliable basis for link budgeting and network planning in structured agricultural environments.

</details>


### [262] [Revisiting and Expanding the IPv6 Network Periphery: Global-Scale Measurement and Security Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19487)
*Zixuan Xie,Zitao Yang,Shurui Fang,Zhaoyang Li,Wenxing Xie,Nannan Fu,Liangyu Dong,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文重新评估IPv6网络外围安全态势，通过大规模测量发现尽管IPv6部署加速，但安全挑战依然存在且结构性问题突出，包括服务暴露、路由循环和LLM工具配置漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IPv6部署加速，但2021年DSN研究仅覆盖三个地区且已过时，需要全面更新的全球IPv6网络外围安全评估，以了解当前安全态势和风险。

Method: 提出响应引导前缀选择(RGPS)策略高效识别高价值IPv6前缀进行探测；进行全球规模测量覆盖73个国家/地区；设计分层LLM暴露验证(HLEV)框架识别LLM部署工具中的未授权访问风险。

Result: 识别超过2.819亿个活跃IPv6网络外围，印度、中国和美国增长371.2%；2.5%可达服务危险暴露；发现450万个易循环响应；LLM部署工具存在不安全默认配置和认证缺失等安全弱点。

Conclusion: IPv6采用率激增，但关键安全挑战持续存在且结构性地嵌入，包括服务暴露、路由循环和配置漏洞，需要持续关注和改进安全实践。

Abstract: As IPv6 deployment accelerates, understanding the evolving security posture of network peripheries becomes increasingly important. A DSN 2021 study introduced the first large-scale discovery of IPv6 network peripheries, uncovering risks like service exposure and routing loops. However, its scope was limited to three regions and is now outdated. In this paper, we revisit and significantly expand upon that work, presenting a comprehensive, up-to-date security assessment of IPv6 network peripheries. To support efficient large-scale scanning, we propose a novel Response-Guided Prefix Selection (RGPS) strategy to identify high-value IPv6 prefixes for probing. Our global-scale measurement covers 73 countries/regions and identifies over 281.9M active IPv6 network peripheries, including a 371.2\% increase (245M) over the 52M reported in 2021 for India, China, and America. Our service exposure analysis shows that 2.5\% of reachable services are still dangerously exposed, including outdated administrative interfaces and misconfigured servers, while correlation with known CVEs reveals recurring software vulnerabilities. Building on this service-exposure perspective, we further design a Hierarchical LLM Exposure Verification (HLEV) framework to identify unauthorized-access risks in exposed LLM deployment tools, revealing multiple security weaknesses caused by insecure default configurations and missing authentication. Additionally, we revisit routing loop vulnerabilities and identify 4.5M loop-prone responses, confirming that flawed routing behaviors remain widespread across vendors and countries/regions. These findings suggest that while IPv6 adoption has surged, key security challenges persist and are structurally embedded.

</details>


### [263] [ZODIAC: Zero-shot Offline Diffusion for Inferring Multi-xApps Conflicts in Open Radio Access Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19610)
*Zeyu Fang,Shu Hong,Huu Trung Thieu,Nakjung Choi,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: ZODIAC：首个无需联合执行数据、仅凭边缘离线数据就能进行O-RAN冲突推理的零样本框架，通过三阶段方法有效识别冲突诱导条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: O-RAN中多厂商xApps的并发执行可能引发冲突，而现有冲突管理方法严重依赖联合执行数据，这些数据在实践中往往难以获取。

Method: 提出ZODIAC三阶段框架：1）不确定性感知代理模型训练；2）轨迹级扩散训练；3）组合引导去噪，实现高效、物理约束且可靠的冲突条件搜索。

Result: 在Mobile-Env平台和NS-O-RAN-Flexric模拟器上，ZODIAC在Top-20真阳性率上比基线方法高出20%以上，斯皮尔曼秩相关性更强，场景多样性更高，计算效率有竞争力。

Conclusion: ZODIAC是O-RAN中首个仅凭边缘离线数据就能进行冲突推理的框架，无需任何联合执行轨迹，为实际部署中的冲突管理提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Open Radio Access Network (O-RAN) enables network control through multi-vendor xApps operating both within and across layers, subnets, and domains, whose concurrent execution can trigger conflicts that are latent during the development phase. Existing conflict management approaches rely heavily on joint-execution data, which is often unavailable in practice. To address this limitation, we formalize a novel problem termed conflict reasoning, which involves identifying conflict-inducing conditions given only marginal datasets from each individual xApp. We propose ZODIAC, a three-stage framework for zero-shot conflict condition inference that comprises uncertainty-aware surrogate model training, trajectory-level diffusion training, and compositional guided denoising for efficient, physics-constrained, and reliable condition search. We derive a theoretical lower confidence bound showing that the compositional reasoning in ZODIAC serves as a principled surrogate for true conflict severity, with the epistemic penalty directly controlling the approximation gap. We evaluate ZODIAC on both the lightweight Mobile-Env platform across all three O-RAN Alliance conflict types (direct, indirect, and implicit) and a realistic NS-O-RAN-Flexric simulator. ZODIAC consistently outperforms baseline condition search methods, achieving over 20% higher True Positive Rate at Top-20, substantially stronger Spearman rank correlation, greater scenario diversity, and competitive computational efficiency. Ablation studies confirm the necessity of each guidance component, with epistemic uncertainty penalties proving essential for filtering spurious conflicts. To the best of our knowledge, ZODIAC is the first framework in O-RAN that enables conflict reasoning from marginal offline data without requiring any joint-execution traces.

</details>
